## ü§î Qu'est-ce que Seedance 2.0 ?

**Seedance 2.0** est un mod√®le de g√©n√©ration vid√©o d√©velopp√© par **ByteDance**. C'est le premier mod√®le de l'industrie √† prendre en charge **l'entr√©e quadri-modale simultan√©e** ‚Äî image, vid√©o, audio et texte.

**Key Features:**
- üé• **Texte vers Vid√©o** ‚Äî G√©n√©rer des vid√©os √† partir de descriptions textuelles
- üñºÔ∏è **Image vers Vid√©o** ‚Äî Animer des images statiques en vid√©os dynamiques
- üìπ **Vid√©o vers Vid√©o** ‚Äî Transformer et √©tendre des vid√©os existantes
- üéµ **Pilot√© par Audio** ‚Äî G√©n√©rer des vid√©os pilot√©es par une entr√©e audio
- üìê **R√©solution jusqu'√† 1080p**, dur√©e de 4-15 secondes
- üîä **Doublage et scoring automatiques** ‚Äî Voix off et musique de fond automatiques

### Horror Short Film Script: The Mirror Glitch

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, three-scene script prompt for a pseudo-documentary (Vlog style) short film with a suspenseful, slightly horrific tone. The plot centers on a young woman brushing her teeth, where the reflection in the mirror exhibits a delayed, independent consciousness before glitching and disappearing, leaving the protagonist confused and scared. Requires a reference image of the protagonist.

#### üìù Prompt

```
[Style] Pseudo-documentary (Vlog Style), hyperrealism, fixed camera real-shot feel, natural light, with a touch of suspense and horror. 
[Duration] 15 seconds 
[Protagonist (Remember to upload reference image)] A sexy young woman preparing to wash up and go to bed in front of her bathroom sink. 
[00:00-00:06] Shot 1: Normalcy. Scene: In front of a regular large bathroom mirror. Action: The protagonist is brushing her teeth, mouth full of foam. She makes various funny faces at the mirror while brushing (winking and squinting). Key Detail: The reflection in the mirror is completely normal and synchronized with her actions. 
[00:06-00:11] Shot 2: The Glitch. Action: The protagonist finishes brushing, spits out the foam, and turns to leave the bathroom. High-Energy Moment (Core Plot Point): Just as the protagonist's real body turns and leaves the mirror frame, the ‚Äúreflection‚Äù in the mirror **does not move**! The ‚Äúreflection‚Äù remains in the brushing posture, even smirking and raising an eyebrow at the camera, staying for a full 2 seconds before suddenly ‚Äúscreen glitching‚Äù in panic to catch up with the body's action and disappear. Director's Note: Must create an extremely realistic sense of ‚Äúnetwork delay,‚Äù giving the reflection a feeling of independent consciousness. 
[00:11-00:15] Shot 3: The Punchline. Action: The protagonist, who has reached the door, seems to sense something is wrong and quickly turns back to look at the mirror. Result: The mirror has completely returned to normal, empty, only reflecting the opposite wall. The protagonist looks confused and scared, glances around the room, and shows a horrified expression. The frame freezes on the protagonist's bewildered face (horror movie effect).
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/b4dfa5920ffbe5cafb0bfa2e1c8d5e43/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Horror Short Film Script: The Mirror Glitch">

**Auteur:** [MapleShaw](https://x.com/msjiaozhu) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/msjiaozhu/status/2021777584913363052) | **Publi√©:** Feb 12, 2026

**[üé¨ Voir la vid√©o ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/fr-FR/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=194)**

### Gritty Boxing Sparring Session

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A detailed prompt for a photorealistic cinematic video comparing Kling 3.0 and Seedance 2.0, describing a handheld shot circling two boxers sparring in a gritty gym, focusing on visceral realism, sweat, and stable identity.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Handheld shot circling two boxers practice sparring in a gritty gym, purposefully missing each other with their swings. Sweat droplets, sharp impacts, breathing intensity. Shallow depth of field, practical lighting, visceral realism, stable identity. Duration: 10s. Aspect ratio: 16:9. Photoreal cinematic. Single shot unless specified. Avoid text, captions, watermarks, logos. Stress camera movement: smooth parallax, consistent objects, stable faces; no text
```

### Absurd Comedy Video Prompt for Seedance 2.0: Nothing

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0, creating an absurd, black comedy narrative. The story involves a confident rider on a horse expecting a crowd's adoration, only for the crowd to ignore him and rush towards a steamed bun shop instead, ending with the rider's self-mocking realization of 'Nothing.' The prompt includes specific scene descriptions, camera work, timing, and dialogue.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Scene 1: Galloping Horse + Enthusiastic Crowd Approaching (0:00-0:08, 8 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Main winding road in a Vancouver luxury residential area (wide asphalt road, large detached mansions on both sides, evergreen pines covered with light snow)
‚Ä¢ Subject: A rider in a dark suit galloping at full speed on a white horse, the horse's hooves airborne, mane flying
‚Ä¢ Environment: Light snow falling, mansions flashing past, outline of the North Shore mountains and ocean in the distance
‚Ä¢ Crowd: A large group of enthusiastic supporters suddenly appears ahead (diverse young people), waving yellow dragon flags + ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù signs, shouting and cheering, surging towards the rider
‚Ä¢ Camera: Medium-speed frontal follow shot ‚Üí Switches to rider's perspective (POV), crowd getting closer
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Climax continues, the rider smiles confidently, preparing to pull the reins (hand already raised towards the reins, relaxed posture, corner of the mouth upturned)
Scene 2: Reversal‚ÄîCrowd Passes Straight Through, Ignoring the Rider (0:08-0:14, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Same road, a Chinese steamed bun shop appears around the corner (sign ‚ÄúQingfeng Baozi Shop,‚Äù warm lighting, simple plastic tables and chairs in the outdoor area, steam rising)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The rider is about to wave in greeting, but the crowd ignores him, rushing past him on both sides/around him, heading to queue/surge into the bun shop entrance
‚Ä¢ Action: The rider's smile freezes, his hand stops mid-air, his expression changes from anticipation to shock/confusion (wind messes up his hair, the hem of his suit flutters)
‚Ä¢ Details: The crowd shouts ‚ÄúBaozi! Baozi!‚Äù, yellow dragon flags wave chaotically, the ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù sign is pushed aside; the white horse is forced to halt in small steps or turn sideways to avoid them
‚Ä¢ Camera: Quick pan/wide-angle shot, showing the crowd flowing like a tide around the rider (the horse is ‚Äúpassed through‚Äù in the center of the frame), the rider is left alone in the middle
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Absurd reversal, awkward confusion, black humor climax
Scene 3: Eating Buns and Dialogue Outside the Bun Shop (0:14-0:20, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Outdoor area of Qingfeng Baozi Shop (plastic tables and chairs, steaming baskets, luxury residential road in the background)
‚Ä¢ Subject: Two ordinary young people (wearing down jackets) sitting in the queue seats, eating buns heartily
‚Ä¢ Action: One person takes a bite of the bun, closes their eyes in satisfaction, ‚ÄúAh, so fragrant.‚Äù (Close-up shot of the bun being bitten open, showing steam/juice)
‚Ä¢ Dialogue:
First person (eating while looking towards the road): Who is that guy?
Second person (thoughtfully, chewing the bun, looking into the distance): Nothing.
‚Ä¢ Camera: Medium shot of two people ‚Üí Slight push-in on facial expressions (satisfied + calm), the rider's receding figure is vaguely visible in the background
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Down-to-earth, contrasting cuteness, referencing the theme ‚Äúnothing‚Äù
Scene 4: Rider Self-Mockingly Continues Galloping Away (0:20-0:30, 10 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Wide, extending road in the luxury residential area (straight ahead, mansions gradually receding)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The rider on the horse, his expression changing from confusion to a confident smile
‚Ä¢ Action: He reaches into his suit breast pocket, pulls out a packaged sandwich, takes a big bite (juice/crumbs splatter), then shakes his head dashingly, lightly taps the white horse with the reins, and continues galloping forward
‚Ä¢ Environment: The mansion complex shrinks in the background, the evergreen trees on both sides of the road and the supporters (now stopped) can only be seen waving from afar, the Vancouver-style mountain and sea skyline in the distance (snowy and hazy)
‚Ä¢ Details: The white horse's tail swings, hoof prints are left on the lightly snow-covered road, the bite mark on the sandwich is clear, the rider smiles confidently
‚Ä¢ Camera: From close-up (sandwich bite detail) ‚Üí Slowly pulls back to an extreme long shot, low-angle perspective, emphasizing the ‚Äúdon't care‚Äù sense of isolated heroism; finally fades out
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Self-mocking yet dashing, heroic and unrestrained, symbolic ending (‚ÄúNothing‚Äù can still move forward)
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/31130a874536d7d55a28e682d4cf4105/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Absurd Comedy Video Prompt for Seedance 2.0: Nothing">

**Auteur:** [John](https://x.com/john87445528) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2021706240272069021) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

### Surreal Battlefield Ronin Action Scene

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, multi-shot prompt for Seedance 2.0 describing a surreal, high-action battlefield scene in the sky, featuring a masked ronin pursued by a colossal winged beast whose chest is a vortex of storm clouds. The prompt includes specific camera movements, technical details (720p, 16:9, 15 seconds), and a dramatic finale.

#### üìù Prompt

```
A surreal battlefield in the sky: floating rock islands drifting through a thunderstorm, clouds swirling below like an ocean. The masked ronin dashes across the drifting platforms, pursued by a colossal winged beast whose chest is a swirling vortex of storm clouds and lightning. The camera hurtles from island to island, struggling to keep up as rocks tilt, spin, and crumble away beneath them. Every wingbeat sends shockwaves through the air, shaking the frame and blowing debris and rain straight into the viewer‚Äôs face. Rapid handheld cuts capture the ronin leaping impossible gaps, sword carving arcs of light that briefly cut through the darkness. The finale shows the camera diving behind him as he jumps off the last crumbling rock, riding a bolt of lightning directly into the monster‚Äôs chest vortex with a final, all-or-nothing slash that explodes the storm from within and clears the sky in a blinding flash.

720p
16:9
15 seconds
```

### The Flash Director's Prompt

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, multi-part 'Director‚Äôs Prompt' used with Seedance 2.0 via ChatCut, describing a complex, dynamic, and cinematic sequence featuring The Flash accelerating and creating a time portal.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Opening Shot:
Extreme close-up on The Flash‚Äôs boots touching wet asphalt at night. Raindrops freeze midair as time slows. Golden lightning begins to crawl over his suit, crackling softly.
Camera: Low-angle, slow push-in.
As he leans forward, the world stretches and distorts. On the beat, he launches. The camera snaps into pursuit as he explodes forward in a blinding burst of red and gold lightning, tearing through the city streets. Buildings smear into light trails, traffic lights become streaks of color, thunder rolling underneath the sound design.

DIRECTOR‚ÄôS PROMPT ‚Äî PART 2

The Flash accelerates beyond the city, racing across highways, deserts, and oceans in seconds. The curvature of the Earth becomes visible as clouds rip apart beneath him.
Camera: Dynamic tracking shot with heavy motion blur, lightning arcing outward like veins of energy.
Time fractures ‚Äî day and night collapse into one continuous run. As he reaches maximum velocity, the lightning intensifies into near-white brilliance. He vanishes in a final thunderous flash, leaving only scorched air, fading electricity, and silence.

DIRECTOR‚ÄôS PROMPT ‚Äî PART 3

A low, resonant hum builds. The air ahead fractures like glass. A circular portal forms ‚Äî ancient, unstable ‚Äî glowing with swirling light and dust, as if time itself is being torn open.
```

### Chaos in a Maasai Village


### Demon Slayer Live-Action Battle Prompt for Seedance 2.0

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, high-energy video prompt for Seedance 2.0 generating a 15-second live-action adaptation of a Demon Slayer-style battle (Water Breathing vs. Thunder Breathing). The prompt specifies the style (Hollywood live-action manga adaptation, dark samurai, 4K, extreme quick cuts, particle light effects), the setting (misty forest at night), and three distinct shots detailing the characters' actions, power-up sequences, and the final clash.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Live-Action Manga Adaptation ¬∑ Breathing Style Decisive Battle (15 seconds ¬∑ Ultra-Burning Special Effects Version)
„ÄêCore Focus„Äë: Water Breathing (Blue Water Dragon) VS Thunder Breathing (Golden Lightning), live-action extreme speed duel.
„ÄêStyle„Äë: Hollywood live-action manga adaptation film quality, dark samurai style, 4K ultra-clear, extreme quick cuts, particle light effects explosion, no gore.
„ÄêDuration„Äë: 15 seconds
„ÄêScene„Äë: Misty forest under the moonlight, muddy ground, falling leaves.
[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Water Melody Prelude ¬∑ Starting Form (Sense of Charging)
Visuals: A young samurai wearing a green and black checkered haori (jacket), lowers his center of gravity under the moonlight, holding his sword with both hands.
Action: He takes a deep breath, and the surrounding air instantly solidifies. As he draws his sword, a giant blue water dragon, condensed from high-pressure water flow, appears out of thin air, rotating rapidly around his body and blade, emitting the roar of flowing water.
Special Effects Details: The water flow has a realistic sense of splashing, illuminating the dark forest.
[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Thunder Flash ¬∑ Advance (Sense of Extreme Speed)
Visuals: The opponent across from him, a blonde swordsman wearing a yellow triangular patterned haori, lowers his body extremely low, taking the stance of an Iaijutsu (sword drawing technique).
Action: The ground suddenly explodes. His entire body instantly transforms into a dazzling golden lightning afterimage, rapidly refracting and advancing in a 'Z' shape through the trees at a speed invisible to the naked eye.
Special Effects Details: Golden electric arcs and scorched fallen leaves remain in the places he passes.
[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: Water-Thunder Collision ¬∑ Final Sound (Clash of Ultimate Moves)
Visuals: Extreme speed head-on collision. The young samurai swings the giant blue water dragon down to meet the attack, and the blonde swordsman, transformed into lightning, crashes into it.
Action: The two swords violently collide in the center of the frame.
Special Effects Spectacle: The blue water dragon and the golden lightning instantly explode, forming a massive water-thunder energy storm that spreads outward. The surrounding large trees are snapped in half by the energy wave, and mud, water, and light obscure the camera. The scene ends in an extremely dazzling blue, yellow, and white light.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/f42542bbe17a09b73c365d33e19770f9/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Demon Slayer Live-Action Battle Prompt for Seedance 2.0">

### Xianxia Animated Film Battle Script: Han Li vs. Wang Lin

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, four-scene script prompt for a 15-second, high-energy duel in the style of a Chinese Xianxia (immortal hero) animated film. The prompt features a battle between the characters Han Li (with golden flying swords) and Wang Lin (with a massive cyan phantom hand and a black sphere of destruction), emphasizing ultra-fine 3D CG rendering and a strong gold/cyan color contrast.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Chinese Xianxia animated film style, ultra-fine 3D CG rendering, 15-second high-energy duel sequence, strong contrast between gold and cyan dual tones. 0-3 seconds: Extreme long shot, two streams of light rapidly clash from both sides of the frame in chaotic void‚Äîon the left, faintly visible in the golden light is a middle-aged cultivator in a cyan-gray Daoist robe, his face calm as water, holding a small green sword, who is Han Li; on the right, in the cyan-black malevolent aura, a thin man in white hair and black robes stands with his hands behind his back, his eyes deep as an ancient well, surrounded by world-destroying energy, who is Wang Lin. The two face each other from afar, the void cracking due to the collision of their auras, accompanied by a low thunderous roar. 4-8 seconds: Han Li forms a hand seal to activate the Azure Bamboo Cloud-Swarm Swords, seventy-two flying swords transform into a golden storm of sword rain sweeping away; Wang Lin points with his right hand, and a giant cyan phantom hand that covers the sky condenses behind him. The giant hand slaps down against the sword rain, and the moment the sword energy and palm force collide, a golden and cyan energy torrent erupts, the shockwave spreading in all directions and tearing the void, accompanied by the sound of metal collision and space shattering. 9-12 seconds: Freeze frame slow motion, a golden phantom of ten thousand Buddhas appears behind Han Li, his eyes shining with golden light, and the Ten Thousand Swords Return to the Origin condense into a hundred-zhang golden sword light slashing down; a hint of madness flashes in Wang Lin's eyes, and he growls, "If heaven does not tolerate me, I shall defy it!" He raises his right hand high, and a rotating black sphere condenses in his palm, emitting destructive energy that twists space. The two ultimate forces collide head-on, and time seems to stand still. 13-15 seconds: Massive energy explosion, the screen is swallowed by white light and slowly dissipates. In the smoke and dust, two figures stand back-to-back in the shattered void, their robes tattered, both panting. Han Li speaks faintly, "I admire your heaven-defying technique," and a slight smile appears on Wang Lin's lips. The sound effects converge into the crisp sound of void fragments falling and a fading wind sound.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d3faf2fcba6019e82251b07ba8c7def0/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Xianxia Animated Film Battle Script: Han Li vs. Wang Lin">

**Auteur:** [ÊùæÊûúÂÖàÊ£Æ](https://x.com/songguoxiansen) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2021591223505662201) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

### Sci-Fi Transformation Short Film Script: Awakening Future

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, six-scene script prompt for a high-impact, cinematic short film titled 'Awakening Future.' The video features a dramatic transformation from an ancient, pure salt lake goddess into a neon-lit cyberpunk warrior, emphasizing IMAX quality, high contrast, and ARRI Alexa 65mm aesthetics.

#### üìù Prompt

```
[Film Setting] Cinematic quality, IMAX aspect ratio, ARRI Alexa 65mm, high contrast, cyberpunk aesthetic, 8K resolution.

[Core Concept] Space-time folding. Instantaneous awakening from an ancient, pure Salt Lake Goddess to a neon warrior in a future city.

Shot 1: Wide shot, slow push-in. The scene is extremely still. A girl in red and white ethnic attire, wearing silver ornaments, stands on the mirror-like white salt lake. The sunlight is sacred, the background is continuous snow-capped mountains, the wind blows her clothes, full of divinity.

Shot 2: Extreme Close-up (ECU), match cut. The camera rapidly pushes into the girl's eyes. Her pupils instantly dilate, reflecting backward digital streams and blue data light effects.

Shot 3: Jump cut, glitch art interference. The screen is instantly torn by intense neon light. The white salt lake background instantly transforms into a flickering holographic billboard of a cyber city on a rainy night.

Shot 4: Medium shot, low-angle upward view. Visual impact. She still stands in the center of the frame, but her ethnic robe has changed into high-tech reflective functional clothing. The original silver headpiece has become metallic flowing light headphones.

Shot 5: Close-up, light and shadow flow. Rain falls on her face, reflecting pink and purple neon lights. She gives a cold smile to the camera, reaches out to put on goggles, and her aura is fully unleashed.

Shot 6: Extreme long shot, freeze frame. She stands on top of a skyscraper overlooking the entire steel jungle, with a giant holographic projection of a whale swimming behind her. Subtitle: ‚ÄúAwakening Future.‚Äù

Duration: 10 seconds | Style: Top Hollywood commercial film | Visual Impact: Extremely strong
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8481812975fae64af863d524150128b0/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Sci-Fi Transformation Short Film Script: Awakening Future">

**Auteur:** [John](https://x.com/johnAGI168) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/johnAGI168/status/2021577731826213121) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

### Urban Fantasy Short Drama Prompt for Seedance 2.0: Good Luck Arrives

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene short drama script prompt for Seedance 2.0, generating an urban fantasy video titled 'Good Luck Arrives.' The prompt specifies the vertical aspect ratio (9:16), style (cinematic, high clarity, particle effects, healing), character designs (an anxious office worker and a tall 'Goddess of Luck'), and six specific camera shots with dialogue and magical transformations.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Prompt Type: Short Drama Storyboard/Video Generation
Aspect Ratio: 9:16 (Vertical Screen)
Visual Style: Urban Fantasy, transition from reality to virtual, high clarity, cinematic lighting, particle effects, healing.
„ÄêCharacter Settings„Äë
Male Lead: Wearing a dark blue suit, originally anxious expression, average height, representing the ‚Äúworker‚Äù in the real world.
Female Lead: Wearing a white T-shirt and shorts, extremely tall, braided hair, radiating a soft white halo, representing the high-dimensional ‚ÄúGoddess of Luck.‚Äù
„ÄêPlot Storyboard and Dialogue„Äë
Shot 1: Medium Shot.
Content: The male lead stands in a gray office, holding a pile of reports, frowning, looking very stressed. The surrounding air is also gray.
Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúThis project is too difficult, who can save me...‚Äù
Shot 2: Close-up transitions to Wide Shot.
Content: A beam of warm light suddenly hits next to the male lead. The camera pulls up to show the female lead's extremely tall figure. She appears out of thin air, as if stepping out of a comic, with a brilliant smile.
Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúI heard someone was making a wish?‚Äù
Shot 3: Two-person Medium Shot, height difference interaction.
Content: The male lead looks up in surprise (must show this adorable upward gaze). The female lead bends down slightly and gently taps the documents in the male lead's hand with her finger.
Visual Effects: Golden magical particles explode where the fingertip touches.
Shot 4: Scene Change (Fantasy Moment).
Content: As the golden particles spread, the originally dull office background instantly disappears, turning into a splendid aurora and sea of clouds. The male lead's suit becomes brand new and sharp, his expression changes from anxiety to surprise.
Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúFrom now on, I'll take care of your luck.‚Äù
Shot 5: Close-up, eye contact.
Content: The two look at each other against the cloud sea background. The female lead winks playfully, and the male lead scratches his head shyly.
Atmosphere: The screen is filled with pink and gold bubbles, extremely beautiful.
Shot 6: Freeze Frame Ending.
Content: The backs of the two standing side-by-side, facing the dazzling future city night view.
Subtitle Effect: Large text displays ‚ÄúGood Luck Arrives.‚Äù
```

### Cinematic Entrance Scene Script: Galloping Through Vancouver Mansions

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, three-scene script prompt for a cinematic video sequence. It depicts a figure in a dark suit riding a white horse galloping out of a top-tier Vancouver mansion, followed by a crowd of enthusiastic supporters waving flags and 'Nothing' signs, emphasizing speed, luxury, and momentum.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Scene 1: Galloping in front of the Mansion Gate (0:00-0:05, 5 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: In front of the main entrance of a top luxury mansion in West Vancouver (large estate-style villa, stone/wood structure gate, wide driveway entrance, surrounded by evergreen hedges)
‚Ä¢ Subject: A figure in a dark suit rides a horse galloping out of the mansion gate
‚Ä¢ Horse Action: White horse's four hooves airborne, mane flying, charging out at a fast pace or trot
‚Ä¢ Environment: Winter, light snow kicked up by the horse's hooves, mansion architecture clearly visible (large floor-to-ceiling windows, wood and stone combination, multi-story terraces), outlines of the North Shore mountains or ocean faintly visible in the distance, evergreen pine trees covered with light snow
‚Ä¢ Crowd: Supporters on both sides dodge and make way while waving yellow dragon flags (blue dragon pattern + Hinomaru elements) and cheering, holding white ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù signs
‚Ä¢ Camera: Frontal shot, white horse charging directly at the camera, strong sense of motion (slight low angle to enhance impact)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Sharp entrance, unstoppable momentum, stunning debut in a high-end private community

Scene 2: Crowd Chasing Close-up (0:05-0:09, 4 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Next to the tree-lined private winding road in the mansion area
‚Ä¢ Subject: Group of supporters running after the horse (mainly young people, wearing winter down jackets/coats)
‚Ä¢ Action: Running while raising hands, shouting, and pumping fists, trying to keep up with the horse's speed, some almost falling but still chasing excitedly
‚Ä¢ Signs: Yellow dragon flags + white ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù signs are carried while running (signs shaking)
‚Ä¢ Background: Mansion exterior walls and evergreen pine trees quickly passing by, light snow mist or tree shadows blurring and shaking, distant mountains passing by
‚Ä¢ Camera: Follow-up close-up, slight camera shake to create urgency and speed (handheld style or quick push/pull)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Frenzied pursuit, urgent excitement, enthusiastic response from community residents
Scene 3: Galloping Across the Side of the Mansion (0:09-0:15, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Side landscape driveway or extended lawn area of the mansion (side view shows large terrace, poolside or garden, evergreen hedges)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The figure rides the white horse galloping across the frame
‚Ä¢ Horse Action: Full speed running, the moment the four hooves leave the ground is clearly visible, the horse's tail flutters like a flag, snow is splashed up
‚Ä¢ Environment: The side of the mansion quickly passes by (wood and stone walls, multi-story windows blurred), adjacent mansion and evergreen forest on the left, mountain and sea skyline in the background passing by
‚Ä¢ Crowd: Supporters behind holding ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù signs + yellow dragon flags chase but gradually fall behind, some stop and wave and shout
‚Ä¢ Camera: High-speed side follow shot, motion blur enhances the sense of speed (horse sweeps across the frame, background blurred)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Lightning speed, unstoppable, heroic gallop in a luxurious community
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d89b30e92e3e2326f3ca3b50347f5246/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Cinematic Entrance Scene Script: Galloping Through Vancouver Mansions">

**Auteur:** [John](https://x.com/john87445528) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2021545550772924579) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

### Cinematic Wingsuit Flight Sequence

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, multi-shot prompt for Seedance Pro 2.0 describing a cinematic aerial sequence of a wingsuit pilot diving from a snow-covered mountain peak, performing proximity flight through ice formations, and deploying a parachute over an alpine lake.

#### üìù Prompt

```
A cinematic video sequence opening with a serene wide aerial shot of a pristine snow-covered mountain peak at dawn, the summit piercing through a sea of clouds with alpenglow painting the ice formations pink and gold. The camera transitions to follow a wingsuit pilot who leaps from the peak, immediately entering a steep vertical dive through wispy clouds. The tracking shot positions just behind and above the pilot as they accelerate downward, the camera shaking subtly from air turbulence, frost particles streaming past. The pilot pulls into a proximity flight, skimming within meters of sheer cliff faces and jagged ice formations, the camera banking and rolling to match every precise movement. Shadows and light play across the wingsuit's surface as the pilot threads through a narrow ice chimney, walls rushing past in a blur of blue and white. Speed intensifies as they enter a massive glacial valley, weaving between enormous ice pillars and frozen waterfalls, mist and powder snow kicked up in spiraling trails. The pilot executes a dramatic barrel roll around a freestanding ice spire before pulling the parachute at the last possible moment. The camera follows upward through the deceleration, then pulls wide to reveal a breathtaking hidden alpine lake surrounded by untouched snow fields, perfectly still and mirror-like, reflecting the morning sky.
```

### Seedance 2.0 Prompting Techniques and Templates

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A comprehensive guide to writing effective Seedance 2.0 prompts, including a universal formula (Subject + Action + Scene + Lighting + Camera Language + Style + Quality + Constraints), tips for describing actions and camera movements, stabilization techniques, and two ready-to-use templates for portrait and landscape videos.

#### üìù Prompt

```
‚ë† Universal Formula

Subject + Action + Scene + Lighting + Camera Language + Style + Quality + Constraints

Example:
A young girl walking slowly by the sea, hair gently moved by the breeze, natural smile, warm light at sunset, medium shot, slow push-in, stable and smooth footage, 4K high definition, cinematic feel, clear face without deformation.

‚ë° Action Description

Don't just write: walking / dancing
Write: slow + continuous + natural

Priority words:
slow, gentle, natural, continuous, smooth, not stiff

Useful combinations:
slow turn / gently raise hand / slightly lower head / sway with the wind

‚ë¢ Camera Language

Seedance is very strong at recognizing camera movements, remember to write:

Close-up / Medium Shot / Special Shot
Slow push-in / slight pull-out / smooth horizontal pan / stable follow-shot

Example:
Medium shot, slow push-in, stable follow-shot, smooth footage without stuttering

‚ë£ Anti-face change / Anti-deformation

Very important:

Clear face, stable features, no deformation
Normal human structure, natural proportions
Same character, consistent clothing, unchanged hairstyle

‚ë§ General words for quality enhancement

4K, ultra-high definition, rich details, sharp clarity
Cinematic feel, soft light and shadow, natural colors
No blur, no flicker, stable footage

‚ë• Style / Atmosphere words

Healing and fresh / Japanese style / Korean atmosphere
Retro film grain / dreamy soft light / cyberpunk
Minimalist clean / high-end texture

‚ë¶ Multi-shot writing (Advanced usage)

Describe in sequence, do not break up randomly:

Start with close-up of face ‚Üí slow pull-out ‚Üí character walks slowly ‚Üí camera follows smoothly ‚Üí end with a freeze-frame smile

‚ëß Avoidance Guide

‚ùå Intense running/jumping / complex multi-person interaction
‚ùå Vague words: good-looking / very beautiful / very cool
‚ùå Contradictory requirements: ultra-high speed + extreme stability

‚ë® Templates that can be copied directly

Portrait atmosphere short video
A young girl walking slowly in the forest, hair gently moved by the breeze, natural smile, medium shot, slow push-in, stable and smooth footage, 4K high definition, cinematic feel, clear face without deformation.

Landscape atmosphere
Sunset by the sea, waves gently lapping the beach, camera slowly panning horizontally, warm orange tones, smooth footage, 4K ultra-high definition, no flicker or ghosting.

‚ë© Summary of Tips

1Ô∏è‚É£ Write actions slowly and continuously
2Ô∏è‚É£ Write camera movements stably and simply
3Ô∏è‚É£ Must add stable / no deformation / not stiff
4Ô∏è‚É£ Quality & style are added last
5Ô∏è‚É£ Less complexity, more precision
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/63668df8df46ae69a07bf1f8414b6ea1/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Seedance 2.0 Prompting Techniques and Templates">

**Auteur:** [web3Â•∂Á≥ñ](https://x.com/web3naitang) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/web3naitang/status/2021510580440608905) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ Voir la vid√©o ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/fr-FR/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=200)**

### SWAT Hostage Negotiation and Resolution Scene

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, three-shot cinematic prompt for Seedance 2.0 describing a tense hostage situation, including specific camera angles, dialogue, character descriptions (SWAT officer, killer, hostage), and technical style notes (High-shutter speed, handheld camera shake, 24fps).

#### üìù Prompt

```
[Shot 1: Frontal Menacing Shot] A medium shot of a SWAT officer in full tactical gear, gas mask, and helmet. He is pointing his assault rifle directly at the camera lens (breaking the fourth wall). He is shouting with visible intensity: "LET THE HOSTAGE GO! DROP THE WEAPON NOW!" [Shot 2: The Threat] Cut to a medium shot of the killer in a dirty tank top, holding a woman in a chokehold. He has a pistol pressed to her head. He is sweating and manic, screaming at the off-screen officer: "STAY BACK! I'LL KILL HER! I SWEAR I'LL DO IT!" [Shot 3: Over-the-Shoulder Resolution] The camera is positioned directly behind the SWAT officer's right shoulder. We see the back of his helmet and his rifle in the foreground. In the distance (mid-ground), the killer is still visible holding the girl. The killer screams one last time: "I'M GONNA DO IT!" after The officer's rifle kicks back with a single sho and hit head enemy. The killer falls instantly. The girl is left standing, shocked but safe. Technical Style: High-shutter speed action, realistic muzzle flashes, handheld camera shake, 24fps, English dialogue.
```

### Cross-Style Battle Prompt for Seedance 2.0: Goku vs. Monkey King

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0 depicting a 15-second cross-style battle between two versions of Sun Wukong (Monkey King): the Japanese anime style (Dragon Ball's Goku) and the classic Chinese mythology style. The prompt specifies the visual contrast, timing, dialogue, special effects (Kamehameha, Jingu Bang), and the final scene where the two worlds merge.

#### üìù Prompt

```
15-second cross-style duel shot, with a sharp contrast between the Japanese anime cel-style on the left and the Chinese mythology realistic style on the right. 0-3 seconds: Extreme long shot, a dimensional rift descends in the center of the frame, splitting the screen in two‚Äîthe left side is a Dragon Ball-style desolate landscape of red rock and soil, with Son Goku in Super Saiyan state standing hands on hips, his orange battle suit tightly defining his muscles, surrounded by the golden electric aura of a Super Saiyan; the right side is the cloud-shrouded Flower and Fruit Mountain, with the classic Monkey King wearing chain-mail golden armor, a phoenix-winged purple-gold crown, and holding the Ruyi Jingu Bang, standing on the mountain peak, auspicious clouds swirling behind him. The two stare at each other across the rift, the edges of the rift unstable and flashing due to the style conflict, accompanied by a low sound of spacetime distortion. 4-8 seconds: Both shout simultaneously‚ÄîAnime Goku: "You look a lot like me, you guy!" with a youthful, passionate anime voice; Classic Monkey King: "Bold demon monkey, how dare you steal my name!" with a deep, operatic voice. Both rush out of the rift and cross paths. Anime Goku unleashes a Kamehameha wave of pink-blue energy, and Classic Monkey King swings the Jingu Bang in a sweeping strike. The moment the energy wave and the Jingu Bang collide, a style-tearing effect occurs‚Äîthe intersection of the two forces pixelates, flashes, and color blocks collapse and reorganize, accompanied by the angry roar of the Kamehameha "Ka-me-ha-me-HA" and the whistling sound of the Jingu Bang cutting through the air. 9-12 seconds: Freeze frame slow motion, Anime Goku activates Ultra Instinct, his body shrouded in silver-gray aura, his eyes turning calm silver-gray, moving like lightning to flash behind Classic Monkey King; Classic Monkey King's Fiery Eyes and Golden Gaze suddenly light up with golden-red light, his body transforms into a shadow clone using the Heaven and Earth Law‚Äîhis body swells to a hundred zhang (hundreds of feet) in size, and the Jingu Bang in his hand simultaneously enlarges like a pillar supporting the sky, smashing down directly. 13-15 seconds: The silver-gray aura's rapid punches and the sky-supporting Jingu Bang collide head-on in the center of the frame. The shockwave tears the dimensional rift, and both the Dragon Ball wasteland and Flower and Fruit Mountain are swallowed by the energy torrent. After a flash of white light, the smoke and dust clear, and two figures stand back-to-back in the merged new world‚Äîa strange terrain blending mountains and wasteland. Anime Goku scratches his head and laughs, saying, "What powerful strength, let's fight again next time," and Classic Monkey King lightly strokes his monkey whiskers and nods, "I'll find another place to play next time." The sound effects conclude with the hearty laughter of both and a fading wind sound.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/df705fc2634dbd418f2a891e43ea8210/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Cross-Style Battle Prompt for Seedance 2.0: Goku vs. Monkey King">

**Auteur:** [ÊùæÊûúÂÖàÊ£Æ](https://x.com/songguoxiansen) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2021508348433301926) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ Voir la vid√©o ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/fr-FR/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=190)**

### Rugby Match: Humans vs. Silverback Gorillas

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, hyper-realistic prompt comparing Kling 3.0 and Seedance 2.0, describing a live-action sports broadcast of a rugby match where human players tackle a massive silverback gorilla running with the ball.

#### üìù Prompt

### Wuxia Duel in Bamboo Forest Video Prompt for Seedance 2.0

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-shot video prompt for Seedance 2.0 generating a classic Wuxia (martial arts) film scene titled 'Bamboo Ink Remnants.' The prompt specifies the style (high-speed cinematography, cold tones), characters (a swordswoman in red and a scholar in white with modern glasses), the setting (a deep green bamboo forest), and six specific camera shots with corresponding actions and timing.

#### üìù Prompt

```
„ÄêStyle„ÄëClassic Wuxia Film - „ÄêBamboo Ink Remnants„Äë, High-speed Cinematography, combination of live-action and CG, strong visual impact, fast pace, using ‚Äúcold tones‚Äù to enhance the depth of the bamboo forest. „ÄêDuration„Äë15 seconds „ÄêCharacters„ÄëA swordswoman in a fiery red dress, movements as light as a swallow, sharp sword energy. This is not a life-and-death struggle, but a contest of speed and precision. „Äê00:00 - 00:01„ÄëShot 1: Close-up, „ÄêAction„ÄëTwo cold-shining long swords collide violently against the bamboo forest background, sparks fly, strong metallic texture. Sword blades clash, slow motion, metallic luster. „Äê00:01 - 00:03„ÄëShot 2: Medium Shot, „ÄêAction„ÄëThe woman in red quickly spins to dodge, the man in white chases with his sword. The background is a dense emerald bamboo forest, with falling leaves. Wuxia action, graceful, sense of speed, Hanfu. „Äê00:03 - 00:05„ÄëShot 3: Low Angle, „ÄêAction„ÄëThe woman in red slides backward, dodging a fatal blow close to the ground. Dust flies up from the ground, the camera follows the movement. Sliding, thrilling evasion, dynamic composition. „Äê00:05 - 00:08„ÄëShot 4, Mid-Long Shot, „ÄêAction„ÄëThe two stand still in a clearing in the bamboo forest. The man in white locks the woman in red's attack with his dual swords, the sword tip pointing directly at her throat. Stalemate, sense of oppression, confrontation. „Äê00:08 - 00:11„ÄëShot 5, Extreme Close-up (ECU), „ÄêAction„ÄëFocuses on the upper bodies of the two. The long sword is held across the woman's neck. The woman's eyes are firm, the man's expression is calm (wearing glasses). Eye contact, tense atmosphere, detail depiction. „Äê00:11 - 00:14„ÄëShot 6, Wide to CU, „ÄêAction„ÄëThe two pass by each other, standing back-to-back. The camera switches to a close-up, a strand of severed hair slowly floats down in the air. Artistic conception, severed hair, elegant conclusion, slow motion.
```

### High-End Cinematic Food Reel

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A detailed prompt for generating a high-end cinematic food reel video based on a reference image, specifying ultra-close macro shots, dynamic micro-cuts, professional lighting, and sensory details.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Create a high-end cinematic food reel video based on the provided reference image, preserving the exact dish, ingredients, plating, textures, and colors. Use ultra-close macro shots with fast, dynamic micro-cuts at 50 frames per second for smooth premium slow motion, including tight push-ins, subtle lateral slides, shallow depth of field, precise focus pulls, and sensory details like steam, glossy sauce, crispy textures, or gentle drizzles if relevant. Lighting should be professional studio food photography with soft highlights, controlled shadows, rich texture definition, and natural warm color grading with high dynamic range. No text overlays
```

### Northeast China Sweet Girl Livestream MC Short Film Script

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, three-scene script prompt for a vertical (9:16) short film featuring a 'Northeast Sweet Girl' streamer doing a high-energy MC (Master of Ceremonies) slow roll performance in a high-end, cyberpunk-neon livestream studio, set to the DJ version of 'Night Paris.' The prompt includes character descriptions, synchronized backup dancers, and virtual gift effects.

#### üìù Prompt

```
[Style] Douyin/Kuaishou vertical screen (TikTok Portrait 9:16), high-end influencer livestream studio (High-end Livestream Studio), cyberpunk neon light, 4K quality, Northeast MC Slow Roll style (Dongbei MC Slow Roll), extremely rhythmic.
[Duration] 15 seconds
[BGM Setting] ‚ÄúNight Paris‚Äù DJ Slow Roll version.
[Characters]
1. Protagonist: Northeast Sweet Girl, extremely sweet and cute appearance (twin pigtails/big eyes), but dressed in a ‚Äúsweet and cool‚Äù style (pink furry jacket + tight camisole), wearing huge rhinestone headphones, holding a professional condenser microphone.
2. Supporting Characters: Two black-clad assistants (Backups), wearing sunglasses, expressionless, standing behind the sweet girl on the left and right, cool like bodyguards.

[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Sweet Girl Starts the Show (The Intro).
Visuals: Lights focus on the sweet girl's face. She smiles sweetly at the camera, then her eyes instantly become sharp (entering MC state).
Action: Following the heavy bass rhythm, she presses one hand on her headphones, and her body begins to sway rhythmically left and right (Swaying).
Background: The two black-clad assistants behind her synchronously start nodding and shaking their shoulders, movements uniform, creating a strong sense of pressure.
[Atmosphere] High-end, mesmerizing, decadent.

[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Night Paris Climax (The Climax).
Visuals: The large screen in the background of the livestream studio displays dazzling neon words ‚ÄúNight Paris‚Äù and a laser projection of the Eiffel Tower.
Action: The sweet girl holds the microphone with both hands, her expression intoxicated and confident, her body swaying dramatically with the rhythm. The two assistants behind her cooperate by performing ‚Äúhand flower‚Äù movements, maximizing the atmosphere.
[Visual Details] Golden streamers and champagne-colored light spots float in the air, and the lights flash wildly with the rhythm.

[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: Full Display of Status (The Finale).
Visuals: The camera pulls back slightly to show the entire luxurious livestream studio.
Action: The sweet girl gives an extremely cool ‚Äúgun‚Äù gesture (Wink) to the camera. The two assistants behind her simultaneously take out their sunglasses, put them on straight, and then cross their arms, looking incredibly cool.
[Effects] Virtual gift effects (sports cars, yachts) explode across the screen around the sweet girl, and the frame freezes on the trio's coolest pose.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/184c8225e8158c7bfebdfa5180a36205/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Northeast China Sweet Girl Livestream MC Short Film Script">

### Tollywood Action Blockbuster Scene Script

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, three-scene script prompt for generating a high-octane, exaggerated Indian Tollywood action film sequence. The style emphasizes extreme slow-motion, anti-gravity physics, dust, and massive impact forces, featuring a confident hero fighting dozens of goons in a quarry.

#### üìù Prompt

```
[Style]
Indian Telugu action blockbuster (Tollywood Action Blockbuster), extremely exaggerated physics effects (Anti-gravity Physics), slow-motion ramping (Ramp-mo), dusty, epic BGM atmosphere, no gore, focus on impact force.

[Duration] 15 seconds

[Scene]
A dusty abandoned quarry or construction site, strong sunlight, very windy.

[Characters]
Protagonist (Hero): With a signature mustache, wearing sunglasses and a denim jacket, walking with a swagger, extremely confident and dominant expression.
Opponents (Goons): Dozens of thugs in messy clothes, whose main purpose is to be sent flying.

[Scene Breakdown]
[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Divine Entrance and Minions Taking Flight (The Hero Entry)
Visuals: Extreme slow-motion (Super Slow-mo). The protagonist walks slowly, with a sky full of yellow sand stirred up by the strong wind behind him.
Action: He casually waves his hand (looks effortless).
Spectacular Effect: Just the force of his palm sends the five thugs rushing at the front flying high backward like broken kites, defying the laws of physics (at least 15 meters high), spinning in slow motion in the air.

[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Physics Defied
Visuals: Quick slow-motion switching. The protagonist instantly accelerates and rushes into the crowd.
Action: The protagonist delivers a spinning kick. The target hit instantly knocks down ten people behind him, creating a domino effect.
Spectacular Effect: A huge shockwave cracks the ground, kicking up a circle of dust. All thugs, upon contact with the protagonist's fists and feet, are dramatically launched outwards with a large amount of white powder (substituting blood), crashing into surrounding wooden boxes and props.

[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: The Ultimate Power Move
Visuals: The protagonist takes off his sunglasses and gives a charming, evil smile to the camera (Blinking Moment).
Action: A jeep rushes towards him. He does not dodge, but kicks it head-on.
Spectacular Effect: The moment his toe touches the jeep, it is kicked vertically into the air like a toy car, tumbling with parts scattering. The protagonist calmly puts his sunglasses back on and adjusts his hair against the background of falling car parts and flying thugs.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/d44feade87e8a45bc5e5cd7d198a9827/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Tollywood Action Blockbuster Scene Script">

**Auteur:** [John](https://x.com/johnAGI168) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/johnAGI168/status/2021472044295070168) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ Voir la vid√©o ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/fr-FR/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=195)**

![ÌïúÍµ≠Ïñ¥](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-ÌïúÍµ≠Ïñ¥-orange)

### Gothic Dragon Battle Video Prompt for Seedance 2.0 vs. Kling 3.0

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0 (and Kling 3.0 comparison) depicting a high-intensity battle against a black dragon in the ruins of a Gothic cathedral. The prompt specifies the setting, the actions of two characters (a female warrior and a warrior in black armor), the timing for each of the five shots, the fast-paced editing style, camera movements (shaking, tracking), and the final explosive conclusion.

#### üìù Prompt

```
Use the three characters and scene in the image to create a battle. „ÄêScene Setting„Äë Ruins of a Gothic cathedral, leaning stone pillars, twilight filtering through broken stained glass, dust floating. 0-3 seconds: The female warrior advances cautiously with a spear, the camera follows her back. Suddenly, a black dragon pounces from the shadows, its claws tearing the ground slabs, debris splashing. The female warrior rolls to dodge, the spear drawing an arc of light. The camera shakes violently, the dragon's roar reverberates through the cathedral. 4-6 seconds: The black armored warrior rushes in, slamming his shield into the side of the dragon's head, a dull roar of metal hitting bone. The dragon's head is knocked to one side, saliva spraying from its fangs. Quick cut to the female warrior, who leaps up, thrusting the spear tip directly into the gap between the scales on the dragon's neck, sparks flying. The camera follows the instant of the spear tip's impact. 7-9 seconds: The black dragon angrily sweeps its tail, the tail blade severing a stone pillar. The pillar collapses with a crash, falling towards the two warriors. The black armored warrior raises his shield to brace the impact, the shield surface dented, his feet plowing deep marks in the ground. The female warrior slides low, passing through the rain of debris, her spear scraping sparks on the ground. The dragon's wings spread, obscuring the light, plunging the cathedral into shadow. 10-12 seconds: The female warrior fiercely stabs the dragon's abdomen, the spear deeply embedded. The black dragon painfully raises its head and roars, its neck swelling, a red light surging in its throat. The black armored warrior senses danger, sprints and tackles the female warrior, rolling backward. The next instant, dragon fire erupts, a column of flame engulfing the spot where they just were, the stone slabs melting into magma. The camera distorts and warps in the heatwave. 13-15 seconds: Both warriors launch their finishing moves simultaneously. The black armored warrior shield-smashes the dragon's neck joint from the flank, and the female warrior throws her spear with full force from the front, the spear spinning as it pierces the dragon's throat. The black dragon's body stiffens, crashing heavily onto the ground, kicking up a cloud of dust. The camera pulls back and freezes: the two warriors stand panting, the giant dragon lying dead in the center of the cathedral, the twilight filtering through the broken stained glass illuminating the battlefield ruins. Quickly fades to black.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8b85793fe268c9b7659d4689ffa89b47/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Gothic Dragon Battle Video Prompt for Seedance 2.0 vs. Kling 3.0">

**Auteur:** [John](https://x.com/john87445528) | **Source:** [Link](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2021391303259431011) | **Publi√©:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ Voir la vid√©o ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/fr-FR/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=191)**

### Prompt de montage d'entra√Ænement des ann√©es 1980 style VHS

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> Une invite tr√®s sp√©cifique pour g√©n√©rer une vid√©o de 15 secondes intitul√©e ¬´ Never Too Late ¬ª dans le style d'un montage d'entra√Ænement des ann√©es 1980, avec un aspect VHS granuleux, un rapport d'aspect sp√©cifique, un effet de fluctuation de bande, des lignes de balayage et des caract√©ristiques audio de rock d'ar√®ne.
